 narayansami dwaara vidheyak ko loksabhaa main pesh karne se pehle adhyaksh mira kumaar ne vipaksh kii netaa sushamaa ko apni baat rakhane kaa mauka diya
 Sushma objected to the provision of keeping the Prime Minister outside the purview of the Lokpal and said that when the Prime Minister is not exempted from prosecution under the Criminal Law and Prevention of Corruption Act, why is he excluded from the purview of the Lokpal
 samvidhan ke tahat sabhi ko samanta kaa adhikaar he
 The bill provides that the Prime Minister will not come under the purview of Lokpal till he is relieved
 vidheyak main aisa koi praavdhaan nahin he jiske tahat sansad ke bheetar saansadon kaa aacharan or ucch nyaaypalika lokapal ke daayre main aae, jiskaa anna hajaare paksh ne suzav diya tha
 The Leader of the Opposition in the Lok Sabha said, "this is the first time that all the Union Ministers have been kept under the ambit of Lokpal, but the Prime Minister has been left
" mujhe samaj nahin aata ki aisa kyon kiya gaya
 "sushma said," In the bill prepared by the NDA government, there was a provision to keep the post of Prime Minister within the ambit of Lokpal
 yah vidheyak sthaayee samiti ko bheja gaya

 The Administrative Reforms Committee recommended the establishment of the Lokpal nearly four decades ago
 is sifarish ke maddenjar yah vidheyak pehle aath baar yani varsh 1968, 1971, 1977, 1985, 1989, 1996, 1998 or 2001 main sansad main pesh ho chukaa he
 The current bill states that the Lokpal will have a chairman and eight other members
 inamen se aadhe nyaaypalika se honge
 The Lokpal will have its own Prosecution and Investigation Unit
 vidheyak main kaha gaya he ki lokapal ke daayre main pradhanmantri padmukt hone ke baad aayenge
 Also, the Union Minister, Member of Parliament, any officer of Group 'A' or its equivalent, Chairman or member of any body, board, corporation, authority, company, society, trust and autonomous body under law passed by Parliament, Group 'A' Officers equivalent to 'and bodies with partial or full financial control of the central government or receiving donations from the public will be under the purview of the Lokpal
 lokapal ko bhavishya main abhiyojan chal sakane kii sambhaavna vaale maamalon main aapraadhik dand prakriya samhita 1973 kii dhara 197 or bhrashtachar nirodhak kanoon 1988 kii dhara 19 ke tahat manjuuri praapt karne kii jarurat nahin hogi
 The Lokpal will have the powers of search and seizure and powers similar to the civil court
 lokapal yaa uske dwaara adhikrut kiya gaya koi bhi jaanch adhikari aisi sampatti ko kurk kar sakegaa jo pratham drushtya bhrasht sadhano se arjeet kii gayi ho
 There will be a time limit of seven years from the date of the alleged offense for filing complaints before the Lokpal
 lokapal ko police afasaron ko jaanch ke sambandh praapt adhikaron ke samaan shaktiyaan praapt honge
 For running the Lokpal, funds will be arranged through the Consolidated Fund of India
 yah prastaavit bhrashtachar nirodhi nikaay jaanch karne main centre or rajya sarkaar kii madad bhi le sakegaa
 The Lokpal will also be able to recommend transfers or suspension of bureaucrats facing corruption charges
 vidheyak main yah bhi praavdhaan he ki lokapal bhrashtachar rokthaam adhinium 1988 ke tahat darj hone vaale maamalon kii sunwaayee ke liye paryaapt sankhya main vishesh nyaayalayon kaa gathan karne kii sifarish kar sakegaa

 In such cases, a provision has been made to impose penalty ranging from at least 25,000 to a maximum of two lakh rupees
